1c5:["$","li","variational-inference-elbo",{"className":"wiki-topic-list-item","children":["$","$L3",null,{"href":"/ml/wiki/variational-inference-elbo","className":"wiki-topic-list-link","children":[["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-title","children":"Variational Inference / ELBO"}],["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-summary","children":"A framework that turns Bayesian inference into optimisation: choose a tractable family \\( q(\\mathbf{z}; \\phi) \\) and maximise the evidence lower bound \\( \\mathcal{L}(\\phi) = \\mathbb{E}_q[\\log p(\\mathbf{x},\\mathbf{z})] - \\mathbb{E}_q[\\log q(\\mathbf{z})] \\), which simultaneously approximates the posterior and bounds the log-evidence. 215:["$","li","trust-region-policy-optimization-trpo",{"className":"wiki-topic-list-item","children":["$","$L3",null,{"href":"/ml/wiki/trust-region-policy-optimization-trpo","className":"wiki-topic-list-link","children":[["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-title","children":"Trust Region Policy Optimization (TRPO)"}],["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-summary","children":"TRPO performs policy updates by solving a constrained optimisation: maximise a surrogate advantage subject to \\( \\mathbb{E}[D_{\\text{KL}}(\\pi_\\text{old} \\| \\pi_\\theta)] \\le \\delta \\). 21b:["$","li","gpu-memory-hierarchy-and-roofline-model",{"className":"wiki-topic-list-item","children":["$","$L3",null,{"href":"/ml/wiki/gpu-memory-hierarchy-and-roofline-model","className":"wiki-topic-list-link","children":[["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-title","children":"GPU Memory Hierarchy and the Roofline Model"}],["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-summary","children":"Modern GPUs have a layered memory hierarchy: HBM (high-bandwidth global, ~1–3 TB/s), L2 cache, SRAM / shared memory per SM (~20 TB/s), and registers. 21d:["$","li","arithmetic-intensity",{"className":"wiki-topic-list-item","children":["$","$L3",null,{"href":"/ml/wiki/arithmetic-intensity","className":"wiki-topic-list-link","children":[["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-title","children":"Arithmetic Intensity"}],["$","span",null,{"className":"wiki-topic-list-summary","children":"Arithmetic intensity \\( I = \\text{FLOPs}/\\text{bytes moved} \\) quantifies how much compute a kernel performs per byte it reads or writes.
